Invasion
is the first scenario in the Elves route of the
Keepers version
of the campaign in
Age of Wonders
, and the 8th scenario in the campaign overall. Invasion and the rest of the Elves route are available only if the player chose to help the Elves following
The Safelands
.
Story
Rebel Dead
The stench of decay follows where the Undead lurk. Once perfumed with blossoms, forest rots with the smell of waste. Already Highmen armies drive the dead away from Human settlements, sending them looking for an easier kill. Reapers turn the fertile forests desolate with their touch. Inioch is determined to gather his new subjects by carnage. While the Elves prepare to migrate to their promised Evermore, this monstrous king has sent his legions to sever the safe passages through the tangled woodlands. Hungrily, Inioch devours anything living, adding it to his army.
The Elves of Silvanus took pride in their independence. They refused to honor Elwyn or the Keepers. Now though, we are united. I suppose I should celebrate. A century of hostility between Silvanus and Aldor is over, but grave concerns paralyze me. All Undead must be destroyed if passage to the Isle of Last Goodbyes is to remain safe. But Inioch is not stupid, and unlike the Highmen, he knew the Elves -their weaknesses- in a time of prosperity. My hope rests in the changes of this last century and the hard lessons that the Elves have learned since Inioch's fall.
About the Elves
Elves are a race of immortals whose lives cease only by violence. There has never been a time when Elves have not graced this world, transforming burning wastelands into vibrant gardens full of life. Legend speaks of a time when Elves had many gates to their haven realm of Evermore, but now only the Isle of Last Goodbyes remains. In days when death was unknown, the Elves balanced the newborn by those who passed beyond to Evermore. Now, Evermore is viewed by many Elves as the only hope to survival in a world soured against its first caretakers.

Walkthrough
This map depicts a dramatic Undead presence, along with pestilence clouds that move random. The terrain layout, however, is straightforward and simply requires that the player push the undead from the northeast to the southwest. The northwest and southeast corners of the map are not essential but can also be taken to the player's advantage.
Outcome
Sunrise on Silvanus
The forests are calm, and the Elves have set to healing the skeletal remains of their damaged lands. Hope remains high. Travelers from Aldor arrive daily met by smiles and warm food. These Elves are different than those high-minded ones of Inioch's court. Talk bubbles about the long trip which lies before them. If only there were a way to move the Elves quickly across the great expanse of land. Still, perhaps the long journey will encourage some of the Elves to contemplate their purpose. Perhaps some will fight for this land, this home, and what they leave behind.

Meandor Scenario 1: Jungle of Umbura
is the first scenario in Meandor's section of the
campaign
of
Age of Wonders: Shadow Magic
.
Story
These swamplands are filthy enough to make their inhabitants harsh and unfriendly. This also makes the swamps an ideal location for Phobius' prison camps; flying insects and stinking mud keep the prisoners from escaping.
Greetings Meandor. Once you guided me through a realm of death when my own Master, Gabriel, was betrayed by his wizards and cast into the void. Now I must guide you through another hell. With Teryn as my eyes, I see that you have gathered a force of outcasts to fight for you.
Teryn will lead you to a stronger power, a race known as the Syron. Convince them to fight the Shadow Demons. The last of their people are being devoured-fed to the demon hives. They know only slavery, but I need the Syron to rebel. Go! Awaken their killing instincts.
—Merlin's intro
Map features
Wizards
Meandor
(Player) - Meandor begins at the southwest of the surface with no cities
All-Devourer
(CPU Lord) - The All-Devourer begin with cities in the shadow realm.
Items and item lairs
Ancient Ruin
(item: Shadow Key) - Southeast of the Human city of Ruluk.
Ancient Ruin
(random item) - Next to the above ruin
Ancient Ruin
(item: Star Shield) - In the north section of the underground; contains a star shield.
Ancient Ruin
(random item) - In the swamp at the south edge of the surface.
Haunted Crypt
(item: Ring of Balance) - In the swamp at the south edge of the surface.
Item bag
(item: Ring of Levitation) - In the southwest branch of the north section of the underground, near a Hydra.
Item bag
(item: Anti-Magic Ring) - In the section of the underground accessed from the cave directly south of  Ruluk.
Shipwreck
(random item) - In the northeast corner of the surface
Heroes
Morrandir - Independent hero who will offer to join when approached
Walkthrough
From the starting position, an Orc outpost is found the the north, while to the east is a road where the Dark Elf hero Morrandir can be found and recruited. Continuing further east and then north on this road leads to a fork in the road, where the human city of Ruluk is located to the northwest and a shadow portal is located to the northeast.
This shadow portal is very important because as long as the stack sitting on top of the portal is not provoked into attacking, the All-Devourer will not be able to attack the surface. On the other hand, provoking the stack will cause it to unplug the portal, enabling the All-Devourer's forces to attack from the shadow realm, potentially making the scenario much more difficult.
Traveling through the above shadow portal is not required to complete the scenario. Instead, there is an alternative backdoor route through the cave to the southeast of this portal. This cave leads to an underground section, which is connected to a larger section through the spiderwebs at the west end.  Crossing this spiderweb and traveling northwest, though a number of hostile independent stacks, reveals another shadow portal. Note that a Star Shield can be found in a ruin in this area. This underground portal can be used to travel to the shadow realm to complete this scenario.
Since the All-Devourer cannot attack the surface as long as his initial stack on the surface portal remains in place, you can take any amount of time to explore the map and prepare for the next scenarios (such as by research spells and skills, and creating items using an
Item Forge
) without facing any opposition. Alternatively, this scenario can also be completed by expanding into the shadow real via the surface portal and defeating the All-Devourer there.
Outcome
I know that Teryn annoys you with her dancing, but she has great reason to rejoice.  Because of your efforts, the Syron-Teryn's people-are a step closer to true freedom.  They've established a place of strength where they can fight free of demon shackles.
Oh, and Meandor, do not think I failed to notice your new pets.  The Demon Larvae you insist on hatching in the shadows are volatile things. You may be right, perhaps they can be used to shatter the demon's hive-mind, but many wizards have tried this, only to become mindless puppets.
—Merlin's outro

The
Keepers campaign
is one of two options for playing the single player
campaign
of
Age of Wonders
, the other being the
Cult of Storms campaign
. The Keepers campaign presents the story from the perspective of a member of the
Keepers
and includes an exclusive loyalist path that is not shared with the Cult of Storms campaign. However, the two campaign options have shared renegade paths.

Story introduction
A storm rages. Elwyn is dead. Of the Keepers, I heed the call to bring allies to Julia within the Valley of Wonders. Through all the forces of the Storm combined, our cause is right, so I shall weather it.
I am here; I am ready.
A Perilous Quest
Chosen of the Keepers, I heed a call of prophecy, writing a testament of this time of turmoil. Marked by a new star over the Valley of Wonders and sealed by treachery, this time of change portends a new era, an Age of Wonders. I am called upon to recruit an army for Elwyn's daughter, Julia, who fights for the Keepers from the Valley of Wonders. Meandor's children, the Cult of Storms, threw Aldor into chaos, by killing Queen Elwyn. Misled, fixated on revenge, divided and angry, the Elves of Aldor are vulnerable when unity is most needed.
The Price of Peace
Meanwhile, the Cult gathers dark forces intent upon butchering all Humans. As a Keeper, I oppose the massacre of any life, and seek a gentler way with the enigmatic young race. The cost of peace is hefty. Many Elves spurn Humankind, remembering the destruction of their first home, the Elven Court of Inioch in the Valley of Wonders. Still, Julia believes that Humanity deserves mercy from its ancestral sins. And should the Cult prevail, then what? Do savage tyrants and bloody armies disband and return to goodwill? For the peace of all, we fight.
IN-GAME TEXT
Plot
Chronologically, the Keepers campaign begins right after the assassination of Queen
Elwyn
, an event depicted in
Prelude to War
, the first scenario in the Cult of Storms campaign. The Keepers, led by Elwyn's daughter
Julia
, are opposed by
Meandor
, Julia's half brother who leads the Cult of Storms. The Cult wishes to eradicate the Humans who had taken the Valley of Wonders more than two centuries ago, whereas Julia and the Keepers wish for a more merciful approach.
The player takes on the role of a
"chosen" Keeper
, who is an Elf named Elric by default but can be customized in name and race by the player. The protagonist is tasked with raising an army to join with Julia's forces at the Valley of Wonders. Recently, a star had mysteriously risen above the Valley, signaling that change is to come.
Following Elwyn's assassination, the protagonist defends the Halfling haven of Flowershire from Goblins and arrive at the United Cities to defeat Meandor's forces laying siege. At Lyra, capital of the United Cities, a council of Keepers gathers to explore diplomatic ties with the Lizardmen and Frostlings. However, news arrives informing that the Dwarven city of Deepmir has collapsed in an apparent tragedy. The Keepers wish to assist the Dwarves, but the protagonist also has the option of assisting the Lizardmen instead.
Loyalist path
If the protagonist choses to help the Dwarves, the protagonist's forces help the Dwarves secure Delatar, a Dwarven city on the surface taking in refugees from Deepmir, against Orc and Goblin forces. Afterwards, the protagonist secures the mining outpost of Bronnam against the Frostlings. The protagonist then learns of a legendary hall that supposedly housed Dwarven heroes who will return in dire need. Following these legends, the protagonist finds the Hall of Heroes, reviving the legendary Dwarven hero Bormac to fight for the Keepers.
While helping the Dwarves, the Keepers learn that the earthquake that collapsed Deepmir was orchestrated by the Stormlord
Melenis
, who leads the Cult's army threatening the Safelands. The protagonist's forces defeat and kill Melenis, establishing the Safelands as a new home for the Dwarves.
The star above the Valley changes from white to crimson, while news from Julia has arrived informing that Meandor has resurrected
Inioch
as an Undead. Due to the ill portents and the loss of Elwyn, the Elves of the continent intend to leave the mainland for a mythical sanctuary called "
Evermore
," which is reachable from ships via the Isle of Last Goodbyes. Julia wishes for the protagonist to assist the Elves migrate to their ships, but doing so raises the question of whether there will be enough Elves left to help retake the Valley of Wonders. Meanwhile, the Highmen emerge as a potent force for fighting against the Undead. Thus, the protagonist is presented with the option of joining either the Highmen or helping the Elves.
If the protagonist chooses to help the Elves and remain loyal to Julia, the protagonist's Keeper forces assist the Elves of Silvanus in pushing back the Undead. Silvanus had become an independent bastion of elves following the fall of
Inioch's Kingdom
, but has now united with the Keepers against the common enemy of the Undead. Afterwards, the protagonist receives the word from a friend to come to a Wizard's college to learn a spell that allows for the opening of stable transport gates across the world. This, however, turns out to be trap. In actuality, the college has no such spell; instead Melenis, who had been resurrected as a undead, springs an ambush. However, Melenis is defeated a second time.
In order for the Elves of Silvanus to reach Evermore, they would need to secure the shipyards at Trollock Wood, a place in which Humans slaughtered the Elves centuries ago. After defeating the Undead forces and securing the shipyards at Trollock Wood, the Keepers discover that the the shipyards have been already used, by the Dark Elves, to set sail for the Isle of Last Goodbyes. The Keepers pursue the Dark Elves to the Isle of Last Goodbye. There, fortunately, many of the Elves who had arrived at the Isle have decide to forego seeking Evermore for now and will instead fight with Julia's forces at the Valley.
Arriving at the Valley of Wonders with a force of Halflings, Dwarves, and Elves, the protagonist joins forces with Julia. Together, the combined Keeper forces defeat Meandor's Dark Elves and Inioch's Undead in the process, ultimately also retaking the Valley from the Humans. The Highmen, who are revealed to have placed the star above the Valley, also concede and remove the star, but condescendingly entrust the Keepers to "guide" the destiny of the Humans. The remaining races other than the Highmen and the Undead sue for peace, and the keepers vow to rebuild and share the Valley according to Julia's vision.
Canonicity
The Keepers loyalist path, which entails choosing the Dwarves over the Lizards and then the Elves over the Highmen, is the canon story for
Age of Wonders
. However, certain events depicted in the Cult of Storms campaign are also mentioned during the Keepers campaign, including those in the text on the world map. Therefore, such events of the Cult campaign that are consistent with the Keepers loyalist path are also considered to be canon.

Walkthrough
While this scenario has two opponents, Vorsar and the All-Devourer, only Vorsar needs to be defeated to complete the scenario. Vorsar's eventual city at the south section of the surface level is accessible only by traveling through the underground and then the shadow realm. The All-Devourer has a presence in the shadow realm, but his appearance in this scenario was likely intended for flavor only, since he is of a minimal threat (being a squire-level opponent), while his main city cannot be reached by any means.
This scenario contains several notable events and interactions, including the following:
On the third day, Vorsar will launch a surprise attack at your initial city with a force consisting of two Trolls and a Karagh.
If you approached the magic vault int he north that is marked by two signs, Vorsar will send a cryptic warning, "White skin. Red Eyes that see / Black coats with tails, yellow feet / What can this creature be?" Raiding the magic vault will provide the Dire Penguin summon spell, and will also cause hostile Dire Penguins to spawn over the surface and underground of the map.
At the center of the surface, there is a tower marked by a sign that reads, "Raze me!" Razing this tower will change the terrain leading to the nearby inn to snow.
Outcome
We must fight it. If we fail, we become as Vorsar: insane. Your victories distract the great Beast of the Void. The Beast is supreme. Bow before the All-Devourer... the, the, the... I am losing my mind... The souls... Too many to count. They are coming.
—Merlin's outro

Isle of Last Goodbyes
The Elves are ready. Evermore awaits, but before the reward of paradise, the Elves face the possibility of death. Yet, they are not grim, or resentful. Their eyes are wide and bright. Sailing directly north, the size 4 independent city Elrofan is available to acquire early on. Afterwards, the player should expand quickly to find other cities, since the opponent has a large head start on the map. Since this is a water-based map, spells that enable travel over water (such as

) particularly useful. Alternatively, if you have built-up very strong heroes up to this point, a strategy is to sail northeast and attack the opponent's leader right away.

Life Sphere, Episode 1
is the first scenario in the Life Sphere section of the

Story
Gabriel has endowed me with the Sphere of Life.  It was a strange transformation that took much of his energy to complete.  He trembled under the strain as he bestowed the power of life.  Even now, Gabriel's aura fades. Are there greater changes in Evermore? And what of this land?  I must find a people wise in these ways. I'll seek Julia's Elves in the Valley of Wonders.
Even now, Queen Julia gathers her allies. Gabriel wants me to join them.  Elven resentment of humanity is no secret. Too much blood has been spilt. Gabriel is right. It is time to heal old wounds. It is time for the Humans to restore the Elves.

Walkthrough
The player starts with a pioneer, which can be used to rebuild the city of Olhilm to directly the north. This city, when rebuilt, provides a wizard tower for Merlin. The player also starts with four elven scouts. One way of utilizing the scouts is to send two of them through the cave to the northwest (utilizing the benefits of the Haste Berry Tree nearby) to at least flag the mine underground, and potentially also the Water Mill and Windmill in Serena's area if she does not flag them first. From this cave, it is also possible to reach a neutral halfling city (Luimil) north of Serena's starting area. This city will join for 485 gold.
Additionally, at the start of this scenario, the independent heroes Elme and Torgal can be recruited near Merlin's starting position for 125 gold each. Since gold is likely a limiting resource early on, recruitment of these heroes can be delayed until the halfling city is acquired, since acquisition of the halfling city early on will improve the player's economy.
This scenario is a team battle that requires defeating the four opposing wizards. Serena and Julia are allies, but they will generally not be as actively involved in this map as the opposing wizards, since Serena is only a squire-level CPU and Julia's main cities are cut off from the rest of the map by a body of water. Therefore, the player will need to do most of the work in defeating the four opposing wizards by advancing through their territory and forces, likely starting with Nekron to the immediate north.
Outcome
Julia is gracious. I feel a sense of wonder in her presence that outweighs any other influence upon my mind. The traitorous wizards took flight, fearful of Julia's alliance. Tomorrow, we will deal with them.  Tonight, I will rest.
Julia has tried to shelter me from Serena's hostility, but her Elves view me with suspicion. Elven memory is long. I suspect they punish us for the sins of the fathers we no longer remember.
—Merlin's closing monologue
Notes
The Valley of Wonders was previously featured in the
finale
of the
Age of Wonders
campaign. The cities on this map have names that previously applied in the finale scenario of the first name, including the cities Greed, Padstom, Quenril, and Lustor in the central island and some of the cities around the central island, namely Tolcyr, Demeral, Isoldor, Garan Berg, Mugasus, and Scorador.

Life Sphere, Episode 2
is the second scenario in the Life Sphere section of the
campaign
of
Age of Wonders II: The Wizard's Throne
.
Story
Julia is gone! I can scarcely believe it! An Ice Drake stole her away. I was in the Throne Room when it burst through the window.  I suspected Artica, but before I could explain to the Court, Serena set her guard after me, claiming that I conspired with Artica.
With Anon's help, I escaped. Now, enemy wizards approach, but Serena, blinded by her hatred of humans, believes her Elves can handle any threats to the Valley. She thinks I am to blame for all the land's woes. The Elves eagerly believe her. I must escape the Valley of Wonders.
—Merlin's opening monologue
Walkthrough
Wizards
Merlin
- The player begins at the bridge from the southwest, on the run with no cities
Serena
(CPU Lord) - Serena begins at the southwest part of the map, where her main city is located. Additionally, she has a second city with a tower to the north of this position.
Nekron
(CPU King) - Necron begins at the southeast at his starting city of Hados
Anon
(CPU Lord) - Anon begins in the northeast at his starting city of Esteria
Notable structures
4x Ancient Ruin
- Located north and northeast of Merlin's starting position. These ruins are part of a task associated with this quest. Two of the ruins are empty.
Dragon's Lair
- Near Anon's starting city, tied to the task associated with this quest.
Magic Vault
- Near Nekron's starting city
Magic Vault
- Located east of Merlin's starting position, near a watchtower
Heroes
Chanta
(Archon priest) - Will offer to join when the player arrives at the independent Archon city of Standerdam
Walkthrough
The difficulty of this scenario will largely depend on the heroes carried over from the previous scenario. Despite the fact that Merlin is on the run from a narrative perspective, strong heroes carried over from the previous scenario can, in fact, enable the player to easily turn back and capture Serena's starting city right from the beginning (and then defeat her outright shortly thereafter by capturing her other city). By contrast, the lack of strong heroes can make this map much more difficult, since both Serena and Nekron will be after the player.
This map has a special win condition that involves Merlin traveling through most of the map in order to escape from the Valley of Wonders. In doing so, the player can complete an optional task of collecting four relics associated with the Elves, Dwarves, Halflings, and Archons, respectively, and bringing them to the ruins of Trabian, which is located south of Anon's city. These relics are associated with four respective ancient ruins north and northeast of Merlin's starting position. The relics are:
Elven Storm Mail
(+2
, +2
, Forestry, Magic Protection) - Found at the south ancient ruin
Mighty Archon Shield
(+4
, Block, Death Protection) - Searching the north ancient ruin will initially yield the Forged Archon Shield (-4
, Holy Weakness). The real shield is in the Dragon Cave next to Anon's city.
Helm of Dwarven Fury
(+2
, Night Vision, Cause Fear) - Upon searching the ruin associated with the dwarves (the east ruin), Merlin will remark that the relic has been removed. The actual item can be found in the cave next to the ruins.
Halfling's Thin Band
(+2
, Invisibility) - Upon searching the ruin associated with the halflings (the west ruin), Merlin will remarks that the relic is missing. The relic can be found in the nearby cave guarded by goblins.
Bringing the above artifacts to the ruin of Trabian will reward the player with a stack of 3 or 4 units for each of the above relics (for a total of four stacks if all four relics are found and brought to Trabian). Merlin and the relics must both be present in order for the reward stacks to spawn (the relics do not need to be carried by Merlin; instead, they only need to be carried by any hero that is in the same stack as Merlin). Bringing the relics to Trabian will not surrender them. That is, the player will keep both the relics and the reward stacks.
Upon reaching Anon's domain, you will get a message from Anon stating that there is a teleport portal at the southeast of the underground level. Reaching this teleport with Merlin, which involves going through Nekron's domain, will complete this scenario. Note that Merlin himself must arrive at the teleport portal for the victory condition to be satisfied. Alternatively, this scenario can also be completed by defeating all non-allied wizards.
Outcome
I escaped, but I have no hope to regain the trust of the Elves without restoring Julia.  I must go after Artica.  Gabriel's powers are weakening, while Artica appears to have grown significantly in power.
The Valley of Wonder holds many mysteries. These wizards needed the Valley for some reason. Serena cannot hold it, and now they have Julia. While exploring the Valley, I felt another power there, an influence I am glad to no longer feel.
—Merlin's closing monologue
Notes
The relics involved in the Trabian task are all custom items, and are not part of the game's standard set of items.
The sign for the Archons reads, "Dedicated to the Archons, noble race of the high men." This message is a reference to to name change from "Highmen" (in the first game) to "Archons" (in all subsequent games).

Life Sphere, Episode 3
is the optional third scenario in the Life Sphere section of the
campaign
of
Age of Wonders II: The Wizard's Throne
.
Story
A small force of Elves, loyal to Julia, fled the Valley of Wonders when the enemy invaded.  They are scholars, not warriors. Normally, I would ignore them, but they are being pursued by three wizards intent upon destroying them. Do they know something of Julia? Is the conspiracy trying to hide some bit of evidence? By helping them I may gain Elven trust. I may be able to learn something valuable.
—Merlin's opening monologue
Map features
Wizards
Merlin
- The player starts at the middle of the map, with the city of Glaydenne. This city must be defended throughout the entire scenario.
Nekron
(CPU Lord) - Nekron starts with cities across the west half of the surface map, including his main city of Slaugh in the northwest edge of the map. Nekron is allied with both Yaka and Mab.
Yaka
(CPU King) - Yaka starts with one city, Foronsir, at the northeast part of the surface map
Mab
(CPU Lord) - Mab starts with one city, Lobbu, at the southwest corner of the underground map
Notable structure
Ancient Ruin
- South of the player's starting position, across the mountains
Haunted Crypt
- Near Nekron's main starting city of Slaught in the northwest of the map
Heroes
Avernus
(Elf Rogue) - Free hero who may emerge and offer to join the player; in practice, emergence is unlikely if the player has carried over multiple heroes from the previous scenario
Walkthrough
This scenario requires defeating all opposing wizards under the special constraint that the starting city of Glaydenne cannot be lost. Nekron is allied with both Yaka and Mab, but on the first several days, Merlin will receive a message from Yaka stating that Nekron has returned Yaka's champion, Karzen, back to service and a message from Mab indicating that Nekron has pledged to hide her sanctum. These message are clues that defeating Karzen and finding Mab's sanctum will turn these two wizards against Nekron. Doing so is not required to complete the scenario. In practice, however, it is typically necessary to defeat Karzen, since he is a threat to Glaydenne and Merlin's forces in general.
Karzen is a level 21 hero with 20 defense and 20 resistance, making him very durable against all attacks. However, his offensive stats of 11 attack are comparatively less impressive, at only 11 attack and 8 damage. In practice, the ease of defeating Karzen depends on the strength of your heroes carried over from the previous scenario. For example, a carried-over hero who is maxed-out or closed to maxed-out in both offensive and defense stats will easily defeat Karzen. However, lack of a hero with stats comparable to those of Karzen can make the scenario more difficult. If you lack a strong hero to defeat Karzen easily, the Enchant Weapon and Bless spell can be used to boost combat stats, while the Druid's Entangle can also disable him in combat. After defeating Karzen, Yaka will declare war on Nekron.
Mab's sanctum is located at the far southwest end of the underground level. This area can be reached by using the cave entrance north of Merlin's starting city, and then traveling southwestward. The path to the sanctum is guarded by a relatively strong stack of Undead units that includes two Dread Reapers and two Bone Dragons. Defeating the Undead guards and entering the sanctum will cause Mab to declare war on Nekron. The neutral units in the sanctum are freely recruitable, and the sanctum also has a teleport that can be used to return to Glaydenne.
Outcome
These Elves believe Serena rebelled against Julia. If they are right, Serena is a conspirator against all life. She believes Gabriel has no rightful claim in Evermore. The Elves believe that the traitors want to restore an Age of Magic. They discuss Covenants, Archons, Elves, Inioch's betrayal, Human betrayal, and Queen Julia's abdication of the Wizard's Throne to Gabriel. Unlike these Elves, I am human and haven't the luxury of time or lengthy debate, so I go.
—Merlin's closing monologue

Story
Mining Outpost
With Deepmir gone, the Dwarves insist the earth requires time "to heal." They flow instinctively toward their "Safelands," minds fixed upon building in the "healthy" earth. My stomach is rocking from the dizzying flight to the mining outpost, Bronnam. We arrived in balloons to assure that the dwarven mines remain safe. Since the player begins with a respectable force, including Dwarven Ballons which can fly over city walls, it is feasible and advantageous to capture the Frostling cities in the north at the beginning. Julia Scenario 2: Mount Abydo
is the second scenario in Julia's section of the
campaign
of
Age of Wonders: Shadow Magic
.
Story
In times of trouble, the Dwarves headed east and stumbled across the caves of Abydor, where they took refuge and crafted great halls.
Men are not the only beings to mistrust the mystic arts. Deep in the earth hides an ex-wizard and friend of mine. Fangir abandoned the way of the wizard for fear that magic might attract more Shadow Demons. Even so, they materialize in the fissures of the earth. You must show Fangir that magic can defeat them. He must take up the power of the earth, expel the demons, and seal the breaches that plague his Dwarven kin.
—Merlin's intro
Map features
Wizards
Julia
(Player) - Julia begins in the northeast part of the map with one city and three stacks of troops
Fangir
(CPU Knight) - Fangir begins with multiple cities in the underground, and also begins with troops and watchtowers at the northwest section of the surface.
Skulkan
(CPU King) - Skulkan begins with two cities on the surface and one city in the underground. Skulkan is at war with Fangir and Julia.
Arachna
(CPU Squire) - Arachna is present on the map at an inaccessible location. Ordinarily, Arachna will not be revealed during the course of this scenario. She is presumably present on the map only to prevent premature completion of the scenario via defeating the other wizards.
Items and item lairs
Haunted Crypt
(random item) - East of the player's starting position
Shipwreck
(random item) - Southwest of the player's starting position
Item bag
(random item) - Southeast shore of the surface
Ancient Ruin
(random item) - South side of the surface
Rainbow's End
(random item) - South side of the surface
Shipwreck
(random item) - South side of the surface
2x Ancient Ruin
(random item) - West side of the surface
Ancient Ruin
(random item) - Northeast section of the surface, south of Fangir's starting position on the surface
Ancient Ruin
(random item) - Southeast across the river from Fangir's starting position on the surface
Haunted Crypt
(random item) - Southeast across the river from Fangir's starting position on the surface
3x Item bag
(random item) - In the vault at the north part of the underground
Item bag
(item: Dwarven Chainmail) - In the vault at the north part of the underground. Acquiring this item triggers a message from Bormac congratulating you on finding his "beloved chainmail."
Magic vaults
(3x) North of the player's starting position (provides random spells, respectively of level 2, 3, and 4, from any spheres except Death and Fire)
West side of the surface (provides a random level 3 spell from any of the 6 elemental spheres)
Heroes
Bormac
(Dwarf warrior) - Joins during the events of the scenario.
Walkthrough
The initial objective is to make contact with Fangir, who explains that he has forsaken the way of the wizard to avoid attracting Shadow Demons.
Completing this task requires traveling to the underground entrance at the northwest of the surface, and then heading south and then southeast in the underground to arrive at Fangir's main city of Fankeep. In the process of reaching the northwest, you will likely encounter the hostile forces of Skulkan.
Skulkan is a King-level opponent, which is unexpectedly high given that this scenario is given an in-game difficulty rating of "easy." However, his best city, which is located underground and is cave entrance is at the marsh at the south side of the map, is effectively blocked off from the surface via AI-blocking tiles placed at the cave entrance. In other words, Skulkan's underground city will not be a threat to you on the surface, unless you enter the cave yourself (which removes the AI-blocking functionality of those tiles). Still, given that Skulkan is a King-level opponent, it is generally preferable to expand quickly on the surface to deny Skulkan from expanding.
Fangir will be peaceful when you first make contact with him. After making contact, you can optionally offer an alliance with him. Entering into an alliance with Fangir will reveal his underground cities.
Upon reaching Fangir's main city, he will give you the hero Bormac along with one of his cities. He will also instruct you to find a treasure vault located at the north of the underground. This vault can be accessed by tunneling through the dirt to the northeast of the city that was just given to you, and then tunneling another set of soft dirt tiles to the north. Tunneling can performed by commanding a Dwarven Mole (in a stack of its own) to travel through the soft dirt, since Moles have the tunneling ability.
To complete this scenario, you must capture the Shadow Demon city of Ul'cthol. This city can be accessed via a shadow portal located far south of the treasure vault described above. Reaching this portal requires tunneling soft dirt just south of the ruined city at the center of the underground level.
Outcome
Well done, Julia. The mountain wilderness of Abydor echoes with songs of Dwarven joy. No longer does the slither of larvae and the clack of demon claws chill the hearts of these defenders of the earth. Fangir's return to wizardry gives me great hope that this world may yet be healed.
—Merlin's outro
Notes
You will receive an automatic game over if you go to war with Fangir and end the turn at war with him.
Although Fangir is at war with Skulkan, he and Skulkan will normally not attack one another because the northwest area is enclosed with AI-blocking tiles.
References

Story
In a desert, a river never flows the same way twice. Yet, the river Amtar has always found its way through the dry sand in a predictable route, providing some valuable irrigation.
Phobius cannot lose face. He demands unquestioned obedience, and suspects his lackey Vorsar is no longer loyal. So what better way to eliminate a rival than to send Vorsar on the Draconian suicide mission? Vorsar must know he is marching to his doom. This map is set up as a multi-lateral contest, but on the second day, Vorsar will offer to form an alliance against Yaru and the All-Devourer. This alliance will last until Yaru is defeated, at which point Vorsar will turn on you, ultimately requiring that you defeat him as well.

O'neron was once a sage amongst the Syron. They ruled the Shadow World-before it was dark and sickening. They fought the Shadow Demons for thousands of years, until their world was consumed. The Syron served as slaves to feed the demon appetite until they found a new world to devour. O'neron escaped to our world, seeking help. He fled to Phobius. The paranoid emperor accused O'neron of spying for the demons and with much fanfare announced to his people his intention to send O'neron back to the pit from whence he came.
With him as a hostage, He vowed to enter O'neron's Shadow Gate and destroy all the 'new demons.' I suspect he used Draconians, not only because they are immune to the sickening effects of the Shadow World, but because he sees them as expendable monsters

Noble Treachery
is the second scenario in the Dark Elves route of the
Cult of Storms version
of the campaign in
Age of Wonders
, and the 9th scenario in the campaign overall if this route was chosen.
Story
Wayward Children
Already the influence of the surface world reaches down to the Dark Elves in ways intolerable. Three sons of Raven Tharic have risen three armies of their own, claiming Meandor is insane and that his quest to destroy the Humans is suicide. Tharic's entire family has fled and cannot be found. Tharic is Inioch's cousin, and is one of the oldest of the Dark Elves. With Raven Tharic gone and his sons claiming hegemony, Meandor's control is weakened. As an affront to my authority, the three princes have assembled forces of three races that refuse to ally with me.
Lizard Men, Azracs, and Frostlings march toward major Dark Elf holdings. I refuse to let them come near. I go with force to put down these usurpers. The other Stormlords are strangely silent. They claim to have their own missions, but none have offered aid in Meandor's defense. Can they secretly hope that I fail or are they really so stupid as not to think of this as a serious threat? Whatever the case, my quick victory will bring them all in line. My Dark Elves will do what they do best: Teach obedience.

Vandir the Exile

Walkthrough
This scenario has a relatively small area that is fought over after accounting for the fact that the northern third of the surface is mostly mountains, while the southern third is mostly empty land or water, and the underground section is small.
All three AI opponents start rather close to the player's starting position. Notable is that the Lizardmen section to the east is isolated from the player by a river and a mountain range, but contains a one-way teleport that allows them to attack across the mountain range. Therefore, if you have means to cross the river (such as the
Freeze Water
,
Water Walking
, or
Wind Walking
spells) or the mountains (such as
Mountaineering
), it would be advantageous to capture the Lizardmen section early on to stop the attacks across the teleport and to secure an area that is well isolated from the other AI opponents. Otherwise, reaching the Lizardmen section requires traveling by boats, either via the underground lake or the shipyard at the Azracs section.
The three Tharic brothers (Affer Tharic, Hamael Tharic, and Loran Tharic) appear as heroes for the respective AI factions, but not as their faction leaders. Therefore, it is necessary to defeat the actual faction leaders of those AI opponents in order to complete this scenario.
Outcome
One
The air swirls with shrieks. The rebellious have fallen to my might. I pinned the three princes--like insects--to jagged timbers with cold steel spikes. It is only a matter of time before I find their families and force their return, but for now, I have accomplished my goals. The Dark Elves gather now at a steady rate and we move closer to the Valley of Wonders and our only true leader, Meandor. The Stormlords rile their forces with greater zeal and head out to conquer under Meandor's emblem. We are one.
IN-GAME TEXT

Norwood
Scenario information

Underground map
Julia Scenario 1: Norwood
is the first scenario in Julia's section of the
campaign
of
Age of Wonders: Shadow Magic
.
Story
Home of the woodelves, Norwood is the home of reclusive beings who savor the sacred tranquility of their ancient trees and their cousins the Treemen. This revered haven has always been their home, and they will protect it with their lives.
Lady Julia, your heart strengthens me to endure the torture of this void. Yes, I am in great pain, but I ask you not to worry about me. Instead, focus on the troubles facing all people. I sense the Shadow Demons gain great strength from chaos.
That fool, Phobius, who rose so quickly to popularity among the humans, has plunged us all into battle. He must not be allowed more power. Now it appears Vorsar has secretly gathered a force to conquer the Elves of Norwood. He spins lies about the quiet friends of the forest, insisting that they must be in league with the demons or they would not hide so. You must not allow his mobs to desecrate these ancient treasures.
—Merlin's intro
Map features
Wizards
Julia
(Player) - Julia begins in the southeast part of the map with no city
Vorsar
(CPU Lord) - Vorsar begins with multiple cities in the northwest of the map
Items and item lairs
Haunted Crypt (random item) - North of the windmills in the starting area
Shipwreck (random item) - Northeast corner of the map
Ancient Ruin (random item) - Southeast of Vorsar's main city
Item bag (Venom Stinger) - In the south part of the underground
Magic vault
South edge of the surface, west of the elven city of Oakbark (spell: Purifying Water)
Heroes
Oakleaf - Independent hero, encountered in the starting area, who will offer to join when approached. This map has a special event trigger in which the Spirit of Nature will resurrect Oakleaf the first time he dies.
Walkthrough
In the starting area, Oakleaf can be recruited at the Inn in front of Juila, and a Yeti and an Longbowman can be recruited at the camp near the Inn. There is also a stack of Halfling units to the east of the windmill. Upon gathering sufficient forces, travel west to defeat a stack of Vorsar's units guarding the bridge. After crossing the bridge, there are multiple cities on the map that can be acquired by venturing off the main road:
The city of Oakbark is located to the south of the road (and southwest of the bridge). Oakleaf will hint the location of this and two other cities ("My hometown, Oakbark, lies south of this mountain passage...The other two woodelf villages have turned to the ancient Treemen for protection.")
Further along the road, two hidden elven cities can be found north of the road, respectively to the east and west of the Druids Circle.
At the northeast part of the map, there is another independent Elven city that can be acquired. Unlike the previous cities described above, this city does not have a refugee-status garrison, meaning that it requires a cost to join without combat. Nonetheless, it is acquirable relatively easily due to the garrison's small size.
At the north of the map, there is an independent Frostling city that will join if you bring the Yeti from the camp in the staring area to this city.
The ultimate objective is to defeat Vorsar, who is only a squire-level opponent. Along the way, you may encounter an event, triggered at the ruins near the Druids Circle, requesting that you destroy the Shadow Demon city of Ubuk just north of the center of the map. This city is automatically razed upon capturing it. Razing Ubuk is not required to complete the scenario, but the outro narration will assume that this task was completed.
Outcome
Well done, my friend. By razing the Shadow Demon's city, you have proven to his mob that Vorsar is a liar. They know the Elves are no friend to Demons. Now that the sylvan creatures are organized, they will hold Norwood secure from attack by greedy men or demons. It pains me that you and your people must once again pay a terrible price to teach men to trust the good caretakers of this world. I fear it is your fate to suffer the tantrums of hungry, short-lived mortals.
In regards to your worries, I am not sure about the source of the Shadow Demons. Teryn says they are not from the world we call the Shadow World. Phobius justified banning magic in his empire, claiming he would starve the creatures, but they do not feed on magic. Phobius refuses to listen, so we must oppose him and hope that his people will not be fooled.
—Merlin's outro
Note
The map file for this scenario has an unused internal map name of "Shadows of the Forest"

Old Tower

Symon Scenario 2: Old Tower
is the second scenario in the optional tutorial section of the
campaign
of
Age of Wonders: Shadow Magic
.
Story
This crumbling tower is the only surviving monument of the Elves' great Empire in the Valley of Wonders, but a sad one, now lonely and forgotten. Recently, stranger shadows darken its broken walls.
Symon, let us now unlock your true powers. You will come to understand why others fear you. Their fears are not entirely unjustified. Behold a wizard's tower, or what is left of one. Using these structures, wizards can call down the powers of heaven, shred mountains, and drown legions. Teryn and I will instruct you, but it is up to you to decide how to expend your power. We trust you to choose wisely.
This tower was destroyed by the very beings that hold me captive-the Shadow Demons. These creatures use magic to feed upon the weakness of souls. They have eaten countless worlds.  Teryn is one of the last of her world. We did not know this when they first appeared. Some wizards thought they could control the demons, but they grew too fast. They spread like a plague. Now they appear unstoppable.
—Merlin's intro
Map features
Wizards
Symon
(Player) - Symon begins at the southwest corner of the map with no cities. Scripted tutorial interactions will show how to repair the city straight ahead, which contains a wizard tower.
Karissa
(CPU Squire) - Karissa is present on the map at an inaccessible location. Karissa cannot be revealed or interacted with during the course of this scenario. She is presumably present on the map because at least one other wizard is required in order for scenarios in the game to be played.
Items and item lairs
Item bag (item: Ring of Power) - To the west the Inn
Item bag (item: Elven Chainmail) - To the east of the Inn
Ancient Ruin (item: Frost Mace) - In the snowy valley at the northwest of the map
Magic vaults
South section of the surface. This vault provides the Rejuvenate spell, which is part of an objective that can be acquired during this scenario.
Heroes
Natam
(Halfling rogue) - Independent hero who can be recruited at the inn
Walkthrough
After the initial scripted sequence, the scenario opens up for free exploration of the map. There is no active opposition on this map; all hostile forces are independent and not belonging to any wizard.
Next to the initial city is a shadow portal guarded by a gold dragon. In order to gain access to the shadow portal, you must defeat the Orcish forces at the Critter's Den in the northwest part of the map. After clearing the den, you can then use the shadow portal to access the shadow realm, which eventually leads to the east section of the surface. There, capturing the independent Shadow Demon city completes the scenario.
Outcome
Excellent, lad! Now you know my captors. For a moment I sensed the echo of fear throughout the shadow world as you finished off the last of their scouts. I sense you have blinded these demon creatures to your part of the land. For the first time in a long while, they struggle to swallow our world. You have made them choke! They will try to punch their way back into your realm-to destroy the lands you have tamed. Be on your guard, young Symon. Your feats have made you enemies.
—Merlin's outro

Opposition
is the third scenario in the Undead route of the
campaign
in
Age of Wonders
, and the 10th scenario in the campaign overall if the Undead route was chosen. The Undead route is available in both the
Keepers
and
Cult of Storms
versions of the campaign.
Story
Main
Keepers
Cult of Storms
Select a campaign faction from the tabs above to view the corresponding text.
True Natures
The Highmen and Keepers have allied to prevent our advance. A buffer of Human settlements lay between us, the Elves and the Highmen. These Humans will bolster my Undead legions. It is ironic that I should learn more of the Highmen and these Humans from the Undead than from their allies, the Keepers. I see now that the star over the Valley of Wonders is a Highman trick. This war is their creation. Inioch's death was their doing. Even the Cult's revenge is a tool of refinement upon their hapless Human children.
All devised so that one Human, among many, might be elevated from a world of conflicting choices and embrace an existence where more worlds of suffering Humans may be created. But death has prevailed. The Humans chose death at their birth, and will know it now. And we of the Undead shall not pick the most virtuous among Humanity. We shall not subject them to cruel choices without direction. No, we will feed upon them all. All will come. All will know Undead glory. Fear not, my friends. Your mortal torture shall soon cease.
IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
The Opposition
Soon we enter the Valley of Wonders, but first I must lead Inioch's forces through the Human settlements which line the way. The Highmen and Keepers have allied to destroy us. Inioch has told me some of these Highmen, but I care little. He claims they are the source of Humanity. I see a slight physical resemblance, but Humans are decadent and violent, wild and prolific, while Highmen have none of these desirable qualities. They both share an air of self-justification that sickens me. Still, it changes nothing, they shall be destroyed as any nuisance.
I have rid myself of Melenis for now. I sent her on a mission to assassinate the Keeper that murdered her. It was a good plan; I even managed to capture a Dwarven hero that knew the Keeper and arranged for them to meet in a place called Sugarwood. Though devoid of emotion, I perceived that Melenis was eager. Her leprous flesh twitched in anticipation of revenge. If she destroys the Keeper and returns, I will be no worse than before; but should the Keeper prevail, I shall be rid of her spoiled image. Both options please me.
IN-GAME TEXT (CULT VERSION)
Map features
Starting positions and cities
Undead
(player-controlled) - The player begins at southwest with a size 3 city
Highmen
(CPU Lord) - The Highmen begin with the size 4 city Ranniar at the northwest part of the map. The Highmen are allied with he Humans and the Elves.
Humans
(CPU Lord) - The Humans begin with the size 4 city Dall at the center of the map, along with another smaller city
Elves
(CPU Lord) - The Elves begin with the size 4 city Beryll at the northeast part of the map, along with another smaller city
Dark Elves
(CPU Lord) - The Dark Elves begin with the size 4 city Naldor at the southwest part of the map, along with another smaller city. The Dark Elves begin at war with all other factions on the map.

Walkthrough
The player begins with a modest position and may wish to expand east early on to take control of the Dark Elves' cities. Doing so provides the advantage of having a size 4 city that is relatively secure from attacks and is also compatible with Undead in terms of race relations. During this course of this scenario, the player's starting position may come under attack from the Highmen, who start far in a corner isolated from the player but have a teleport near their main city that provides a one-way teleport to the caverns below the player's starting position.
Outcome
Main
Keepers
Cult of Storms
Select a campaign faction from the tabs above to view the corresponding text.
Dust
The husks of seasoned warriors join our ranks. It is not enough. The living are quick, and must be brought into submission. Only our cultivating hand can bring silence to this land. I feel my arms blistering as corruption flees me--as I am sanctified by Inioch's kiss. My vision, which was blurred by emotion, is clear, cold, and pure. Soon I will be worthy of Inioch's power. I will be one with him.
IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
Feast of the Damned
The Undead feast hungrily on Humans. The Keepers have retreated. The Highmen are scattered. The remaining populations will join our great army of dead willfully or not, it does not matter. Inioch has gained considerable strength from this endeavor. So much so that I am beginning to wonder if there will be any left living that I might rule, once this engagement is complete. Still, Inioch would never be so greedy as to consume all the living, else there would be no source for his minions. I will rule them. He promised, so I will.
IN-GAME TEXT (CULT VERSION)
Notes
Melenis' mission to assassinate the Keeper, as described in the Cult version of the narrative text, is depicted in the Keepers campaign scenario
Wizard College
.

Pass of Grief
is the fourth scenario in the Highmen route of the
campaign
in
Age of Wonders
, and the 11th scenario in the campaign overall if the Highmen route was chosen. The Highmen route is available in both the
Keepers
and
Cult of Storms
versions of the campaign.
A
scenario of the same name
also appears in the Undead route, where the map layout and map elements are largely the same but the player controls the Highmen side instead.
Story
Main
Keepers
Cult of Storms
Select a campaign faction from the tabs above to view the corresponding text.
Signs and Wonders
Over a century ago, Humans destroyed the Court of Inioch. Revenge has bred war and contention between Humans and all other races. Now I learn the truth. The terrible Human race is not terrible at all, but it is free. They may choose atrocities and death, or they may choose a more divine path: one leading back to the Highmen. Most importantly they must be allotted freedom for their progression. Humans cannot survive long in slavery; they must be free. Inioch did not respect that. He sought to subjugate the juvenile race, and it cost his people their empire.
Inioch knows the plan of the Highmen because, before he died, the Highmen prophesied of this day. He ignored their warnings. In order to stop that which has been foretold, Inioch gathers the dead, many of which died in the Pass of Grief while seeking to flee Human rage. If races cannot respect basic Human needs, an end will come. The star portends the end of Inioch's reign and the start of a new age. Though the swaying masses of animated corpses appear endless, I will trust in this vision, and by the star I shall conquer.
IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
Death Threats
The Undead have amassed within the Pass of Grief, a place where many Elves died trying to flee the Human slaughter. I have tried to ignore Gabriel's speeches but I find myself unable. He claims that Humans are the children of the Highmen and that they are a necessary part of the Highman existence. He added that the Undead are the cost they pay for life. I don't understand it all, but Gabriel feels great shame for the loss of life that happened here, and this battle is supposed to reconcile the innocent blood which flowed through this mountain pass. It will probably result in more singing.
Inioch has gathered a cloak of darkness about him. The bodies of his fallen subjects serve as the fingers of his grasping hand. If I fail, any hope of resounding glory will also be devoured by this monstrous king. And while I would never tell Gabriel, I have grown quite fond of the Highmen and their children: these capricious humans. So much so that I will endure their choruses and punch through to the Valley of Wonders.
IN-GAME TEXT (CULT VERSION)

Walkthrough
This map depicts an intense battle between the two sides. Rare for a campaign scenario, the player begins with a relatively large force, including stacks with high-tier troops. However, the opponent is also large and formidable. For example, the AI's 100 gold external income bonus, when amplified by the 2.5x bonus for King-level opponents, is greater than the player's starting income.
Outcome
Main
Keepers
Cult of Storms
Select a campaign faction from the tabs above to view the corresponding text.
Highmen Triumphant
The waves of dead break. Their Master hides in the Valley of Wonders. The star over the Valley burns bright. Placed there by the Highmen to bring this reconciliation, the light serves another purpose. The Highmen are solemn, combing the Pass of Grief with care, for the remains of any long dead Elves. They sing songs of release, and plant the bones of the deceased within the ground below altars of solid stones. But something greater occurs here. Each cairn lifts another soul upward and away into a realm of release-another path to Evermore.
IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
I am Triumphant!
I predicted it, just like prophecy. They're singing again. They are out in the mountain pass building strange piles of stones atop ancient bones. I don't think I will ever understand these fanatics. Just trying to understand the Highmen would probably be fatal. My only wish is that we move on and finish this battle, but they wait. I grow tired of these virtues and desire the rewards for my long labors. Gabriel hints at a reward, but refuses to tell me what it might be. I don't care if it's sacred as long as it's valuable.
IN-GAME TEXT (CULT VERSION)
Notes
The Undead version of this scenario uses largely the same map, except that some of the human cities in the middle are non-razed.

Path of Grief
The Highmen wish to enter the Valley of Wonders, but we beat them to the very path that they forged--a ravine where Elves fled and died by enraged Humans. The Highmen watched from their distant places with callous hearts, permitting atrocities in hopes that their fallen children might see the error of their ways. IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
Pass of Grief
I feel only triumph. Though Melenis failed to assassinate the Keeper, I hear he rushes off to the Isle of Last Goodbyes. He won't stop our great slaughter in the Valley of Wonders by fleeing. Highmen regroup, trying to break into the Valley, but we hold the Pass of Grief. Here we must keep them from joining the Humans. Yet we stand upon wounded earth, for the Pass is filled with the graves of fallen Elves, which died when fleeing from the Human slaughter at Inioch's court. The Undead have the clear advantage then. We cannot be stopped.

Walkthrough
This map depicts an intense battle between the two sides. Rare for a campaign scenario, the player begins with a relatively large force, including multiple stacks with
undead reapers
, but the opponent is also large and formidable (the AI's 100 gold external income bonus, when amplified by the 2.5x bonus for King-level opponents, is greater than the player's starting income).
The battleground part of the map includes two size 4 human cities, which can be used to construct
air galleys
, which are useful not only for their combat ability, but also because they are machines that do not incur a morale penalty associated with race relations. Also worth noting is that the Death spell
Animate Dead
is useful on this map due to the number of razed cities.
Outcome
Main
Keepers
Cult of Storms
Select a campaign faction from the tabs above to view the corresponding text.
Fallen Angels
I am numb. My limbs are heavy, but continue to move no longer needing the touch of life. I have cast the Highmen from their heavenly throne. As the demons they cast from their own realms, they have fallen like stars from the sky and cannot stand before me. I am bound by Inioch's chains of power. The laws of death are upon me, but I welcome them. Inioch is just. Inioch is my king. I have only done that which was just and true. By his power will the world will be reformed, to fit his image.
IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
Gates of Hell
The pass has been cleared. Undead minions pour from the mountains and into the Valley of Wonders. I can feel Inioch's passion in my head as a brand of searing revenge burns his vision into my mind-the complete obliteration of Humanity. I have petitioned Inioch for further details as to my rank after the great carnage is completed, but the Undead king thinks only on the moment of the kill. Still, I will have my allies with me from previous campaigns, and they will be my children, and I their god. I will. I know I will.
IN-GAME TEXT (CULT VERSION)
Notes
This map has a caverns level, as indicated by the button below the mini-map. However, the caverns level is inaccessible and is completely blank.
The Highmen version of this scenario uses largely the same map, except that some of the human cities in the middle are razed.

Story
Main
Keepers
Cult of Storms
Select a campaign faction from the tabs above to view the corresponding text.
Peninsula of Sobek
I am amazed at the patience of this race. Sure, there have been skirmishes in the past, but they have suffered great losses, with no champion to return their ancient home. Such a place is the peninsula of Sobek. Once a most fertile spawning ground, the land was lost after a series of natural catastrophes. Before the lizards could rebuild, tribes of migrant races claimed access to the peninsula. Humans, Orcs and even Dwarves now claim pieces of the land. The lizards trust me to do the right thing and return the land to the rightful owners.
IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
Spawning Grounds
For aeons, perhaps before all other races, the lizards sunned themselves upon spawning beds on a peninsula named Sobek. Hatchlings wriggled from clutches of leathery eggs. Lizards grew on rich beaches, building vast cities which were decimated, not by force of war, but by global cataclysm. Their cities lost, the few lizards remaining squabbled while inept leaders fought over sunny spots. Other greedy races, incapable of appreciating the land's significance, have claimed the rich land. It is time these intruders found a new home. I will obtain these sacred breeding grounds.
IN-GAME TEXT (CULT VERSION)

Walkthrough
This map plays as a four-way free-for-all. The player begins in a relatively secluded position in terms of terrain, but first time players may be surprised by hostile forces arriving at the stone circle at the nearby Ziggurat. Shutting down forces attacking from this direction will require controlling the teleport at the center of the map.
This map is also notable for having a large number of item lairs. Unfortunately, transfer of items to the next map will be limited by the modest transfer limit of only 625.

Cost of Victory
So soon, they forget me. I, who saved them at Lyra, am denounced by my fellow Keepers. They see my power, and cry foul for their Dwarven allies. Do they desire oblivion? Where is their faith? Why not trust me? The lack of unity among the Keepers leaves the Lizardmen with doubts. I have proven worthy of their forces, but they hesitate to commit troops to my squabbling brethren. Can I blame them for mistrusting the bad examples of the Keepers? These lizards put trust in me, and eagerly accepted the peninsula as my gift of good will.
IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
Mating Dance
Vigorous choruses of mating calls churn the hot night, as Lizardmen start the work of inhabiting their ancient abode. It is sweet music. Each discharge of musk means more warriors. Warriors which will owe their blissful upbringing to me. The primal state of these swamps leaves me pondering my own condition. The lizard hatchlings start small and vulnerable. Darting amid the reeds, hoping to escape the notice of larger predators, until they can grow and learn. I have long been Meandor's prey, but I foresee change - a time when the hatchling, which was once prey, becomes a predator.

Meandor Scenario 3: Phobian Empire
is the third scenario in Meandor's section of the
campaign
of
Age of Wonders: Shadow Magic
.
Story
The heart of the Phobian Empire is his capital, Stronghelm, a magnificent city, but young; built to Phobius's whims. Surrounded by mountains and forts, Stronghelm is an impressive stronghold.
It is time, Meandor. Phobius draws his fighting forces to Stronghelm City. He claims that the last, great battle is upon them-a matter of prophecy.  He preaches to the end, claiming the wicked will fall, and only the valiant will be spared.
Women and children clamor at the fortress gates, pleading for the safety of high walls. Hear their cries. Ignored and terrified, they await a fate of slaughter. They expect no less. For their sins, they cannot retreat to the Elf Queen, Phobius has abandoned them, and the Shadow Demons skulk about, ready to devour their souls. Free them. Strike at the heart of the illness. Pass over the praying mothers and children; go to their heart. Take Death to Phobius.
—Merlin's intro
Map features
Wizards
Meandor
(Player) - Meandor begins at the lower right with three cities, respectively of the Dark Elves, Undead, and Shadow Demons
Phobius
(CPU King) - Phobius holds cities all across the map
Sahira
(CPU King) - Sahira begins with a single city at the southeast and is allied with Phobius. Sahira is allied with Phobius.
Item lairs
Note: All item lairs on this map have random loot rather than fixed loot
Ancient Ruin - To the southeast of the player's starting position
Haunted Crypt - On an island to to the southwest of the player's starting position
Rainbow's End - On an island to to the southwest of the player's starting position
Rainbow's End - A short distance west of the player's starting position
Haunted Crypt - West of the player's starting position
Rainbow's End - North of the player's starting position, near an Inn labeled "The Drunken Boar"
Rainbow's End - By the independent halfling city on the east side of the map
Shipwreck - On the island on the east side of the map
Ancient Ruin (x2) - West of the independent halfling city on the east side of the map
Haunted Crypt - Center of the west side of the map
Shipwreck - Center of the west side of the map
Ancient Ruin - North of Sahira's position
Rainbow's End - East of Sahira's position and west of Ilstador where Estra is garrisoned
Magic vaults
On the island on the east side of the map, there are three magic vaults, respectively providing a level 4 secret spell, a level 3 cosmic or secret spell, and a level 2 cosmic or secret spell
Heroes
Xulux (Shadow Demon warrior) - Newly given starting hero for Meandor. Xulux, who calls Meandor "father" and is not part of the All-Devourer's hive mind, was foreshadowed in the introduction of the previous scenario, in which Merlin mentions that Meandor has teaching his larvae to call him "father."
Taberu (Human ranger) - Starting hero for Phobius
Mynar (Human paladin) - Starting hero for Phobius
Estra (Human rogue) - Starting hero for Phobius, set to guard status at the city of Ilstador in the southwest quadrant of the map
Luna (Dark Elf ranger) - Free hero who is likely to emerge to join Meandor during this scenario
Walkthrough
Completing this scenario will likely require sweeping most of the entire map, which is filled with cities belonging to Phobius. Since Phobius is capable of fielding a large number of units, the best path to defeating Phobius is likely through strong heroes supported by high level units. In this scenario, the player is given a new hero, Xulux,  in addition to carryover from the previous scenario, and is also likely to receive a fourth hero, Luna, during the course of this scenario. The combat ability of heroes can be augmented by custom items from the
Item Forge
, such as attack items with Double Strike and Life Stealing, and enchantments such as Stone Skin.
During this scenario, Sahira may cast cast Fire Domain with the benefit of the domain of Phobius, since the two are allied.
Outcome
Though you hide in shadows, rumors echo through the Human settlements of a Dark Elf savior who controls Demons and liberates their kind. Phobius is no more. Queen Julia has sent an envoy, and wagons filled with food and supplies. The outcasts return, bringing with them healing and wisdom. It is a strange day when the champions of Life and Death unite. By doing so, you strike fear to the core of the All-Devourer. The Shadow Demons are desperate. We have pushed them to the brink of defeat.
A great dimensional rift has opened in the east, and is tearing the world apart. But all is not yet lost, for we still have an ally in that region -a Syron Wizard, O'neron. Act as a decoy to distract these hellish insects while O'neron helps to save the souls caught in the wake of this cataclysm.
—Merlin's outro

Prelude to War
is the first scenario in the
Cult of Storms version
of the
campaign
in
Age of Wonders
.
It is also the first scenario the Goblins section of the campaign.
Story
Assassination
The other Stormlords laugh and sigh relief. Cowards! They say, I must prove my worth to the Cult. While they hide in shadows, I shall accomplish Meandor's bidding. The Goblins are eager to die for a cause, looking back only to a lifetime of slavery. I will show them their strength, and they will be slaves no longer. I shall record all their exploits, and they will see me as the first god that didn't abandon them. For many years, the Goblins have toiled, secretly crafting a cavern beneath the Aldorian channel.
I will raise an army of Goblins and strike against the queen of Aldor's Elves. The mission is simple: Assassinate Elwyn, a key leader among the Keepers. The other Stormlords are loath to strike against her, believing her palace to be impregnable. So while they cower, I will finish Meandor's scheme. Upon the isle, the Keepers shelter a village of Goblin refugees, naively believing they can change their feral nature. The fools now harbor more spies for the Cult of Storms than we could have hoped to place and when we appear, the village will join our assassination goal.
About the Goblins
From birth, Goblins endure slavery, whether by their own kind or by bully races. They are nasty and clever, employing all sorts of deviant methods to compensate for their small physiques in battle. Though greedy, they are easily intimidated and fight for little more than the crack of a whip. Goblin foot-soldiers use long spears to get the first strike on enemies. Others employ poisoned darts and blowguns. Frail and worthless members of Goblin society are given the task of delivering explosive bundles which can be used to destroy walls and enemies with devastating effectiveness.
IN-GAME TEXT
Map layout
Starting positions and cities
Goblins
(player-controlled) - The player begins in a section of the caverns with a well-sized force, but no cities.
Goblins
(CPU Squire) - The opponent begins with five cities, including the 3-hex city Aldor, which is in the north half of the isle and where the Elf leader
Elwyn
is located, and the 4-hex city Milani at the northeast on the mainland.
Notable structures
Monster Lair
(low item value) - Southwest edge of the isle
Heroes
CPU leaders: Elwyn (Elves)
Walkthrough
The player begins with no cities, but has a well-sized force in a section of the caverns. The player's initial force includes a
Goblin Big Beetle
, which has the
tunneling
ability that allows for clearing paths in the underground dirt. (Note: in order to tunnel through soft dirt, the beetle must be by itself and not in a stack with other units that cannot tunnel.)
This scenario is completed by defeating the Elf leader Elwyn in battle. The fastest and most direct path to victory is to attack Aldor, where Elwyn leader is usually located, as quickly as possible. This would entail gathering all starting forces to exit at the northwest exit of the caverns, obtaining the independent city just outside of the caverns, and heading straight to Aldor. If the Elwyn is inside the city walls, you can take advantage of your beetle's
wall crushing
and your
Orc Assassins
'
wall climbing
. Elf cities captured along the way can be looted to maintain a positive gold balance to avoid the possibility of desertion. If the march towards Aldor is done quickly, the AI will not be able to muster a force a strong as the player's starting force, regardless of the campaign's difficulty setting.
Alternatively, a slower but steadier route would be to allocate part of the starting force to exit the south cavern exit and capture Milani (the 4-hex city in the northeast) as quickly as possible. Holding this city would provide a significant boost to gold income, as well as denying the opponent a large part of its income and the ability to train higher tier units.
In general, the setup of the map, particularly the player's strong starting force but lack of starting cities, suggests aggressively moving against either Aldor or Milani as quickly as possible. Otherwise, not expanding quickly enough may result in a situation in which the AI opponent becomes stronger and stronger as the scenario progresses. After completing this scenario, the player must choose between one of two routes, which will determine the next scenario that is played.
Outcome
The Toad Queen is Dead
Julia should thank me. By slaying her mother, she can claim to rule Aldor, though Meandor is the true heir. History cannot forget me. I have sent the Goblins scattering across the countryside. Mobs of vengeful Elves stalk my decoys. The forces of Aldor scatter, while I move to the next phase of Meandor's plan to cripple the Keepers. The Halfling United Cities are now under siege, but those besieging are morons. Without my help they will fail. Time is short. I debate whether to follow the established Northern Trade Route, or a subterranean path beneath the impeding mountains.
IN-GAME TEXT
Notes
The events of this scenario serve as a backstory and prologue for the
Keepers campaign
.

Julia Scenario 3: Sanctuary Woods
is the third scenario in Julia's section of the
campaign
of
Age of Wonders: Shadow Magic
.
Story
South of Norwood lie the Sanctuary Woods, an even older forest, where the trees themselves have grown tired of the world and its inhabitant's squabbles. Also a refuge for many shady creatures and outcasts.
Tales of your victories race across the land. Rumors abound about the glorious return of Queen Julia. Your forests are sanctuary to those fleeing the tyranny of Phobius and the terror of the Shadow Demons. I fear that enmity between the races will flare. Phobius uses those differences to destroy.
You are the only wizard qualified to juggle the sensitivities of so many different beings. Beware of Phobius. He will seek the opportunity to prove that any attempt to keep the peace is in vain. He will try to prove that you are weak, and will justify his brutality as truth. Expose him as a fraud.
—Merlin's intro

Heroes
This scenario has a large number of
free heroes
that can emerge. These heroes are: Arcos, Avernus, Bogga, Chanta, Chucky, Danah, Dragor, Eklo, Elme, Fredric, Grar, Grogmir, Jack, Jafsar, Jattah, Karzen, Kaskar, Khitan, Laladria, Lilly, Petrog, Tyltha, Sanra, Shenga, SIra, Tengar, Torgal, Tsi Iri, Wazzz, and Ymbria.
Walkthrough
This is a multi-lateral scenario with open-ended diplomacy. The player has the benefit of being allied with Fangir at the beginning. Marinus, when first contacted, will offer peace, after which it is generally very easy to acquire an alliance with him through the diplomacy interface. Phobius is hostile and is the highest ranked (King) CPU wizard.
Completing this scenario requires defeating all non-allied wizards under allied victory conditions. Conventional allied victory has two requirements: (1) all remaining wizards are allied with you, and (2) those remaining wizards are also allied with each other. This map has a special victory condition that negates the second requirement if you are allied with all remaining wizards at the exact moment that one of the CPU wizards is defeated (in other words, if there is exactly one remaining non-allied CPU wizard, that wizard must be defeated instead of allied with, in order to win).
Outcome
You have humiliated Phobius! The forestlands remain a shelter for those flocking to freedom. Sure, the races of the land squabbled, but you have proven to them all that Phobius is not invincible, and his stony rhetoric cracks when challenged.
I must now ask you to do something difficult.  You must remain here for a time. Promise me you will not try to find me. I know you. Trust me in this. There is too much fear in the world. Already your deeds reverberate in all the minds of the people. I need you visible. You must gather in every outcast. The Shadow Demons must be weakened. I promise I shall seek your help again. Until then, Noble Queen, remain safe, not for your own sake, but for the sake of this world.
—Merlin's outro

Serpent River
is the third scenario in the Lizardmen route of the
campaign
in
Age of Wonders
, and the 6th scenario in the campaign overall if the Lizardmen route was chosen. The Lizardmen route is an option available in both the
Keepers
and

Story
Main
Keepers
Cult of Storms
Select a campaign faction from the tabs above to view the corresponding text.
Coils of Serpent River
The Lizardmen promise complete fidelity after this last mission. My brethren will soon have no choice but to concede my points. The lizards ask that I deliver unto them a large expanse of the Serpent River. Traditionally, the river was one of trade from Inioch's Elves to the United Cities, but since Inioch's fall, the river harbors Azrac pirates, and myriad other marauders, out to profit upon the lush waterway. Clearly, the river needs to be claimed by a force capable of directing it responsibly. Lizardmen qualify, and have promised to maintain the river with honor.
IN-GAME TEXT (KEEPERS VERSION)
Prospecting the Serpent River
Since Inioch was deposed nearly every race from Azrac pirates to self-righteous Elves have sought control of the Serpent River. It is only natural the lizards lust after the twisted waterway. Regulating passage of merchant vessels would be a fine resource. What better species to monitor the safe travel of vessels, than the Lizardmen? Unfortunately a few troublemakers don't see it as clearly as I do, and so I will need to clear the surrounding jungle of dissenters, before the lizards can claim this new enterprise. I am more than happy to indulge this favor, for a price.
IN-GAME TEXT (CULT VERSION)

Walkthrough
This map has 8 total factions that begin as neutrals to one another, resulting in a large free-for-all. Since allied victory is not enabled, all of the 7 other factions must be defeated in order to complete this scenario. The map's terrain and layout are as expected from the name. Besides having the ability to traverse water easily, Lizardmen can also take advantage of the fact that initial race relations are neutral or better with all other factions on this map (besides undead).

No longer will my brethren regard the Lizardmen as savage monsters to be ignored in the swamp. Their settlements now grow unmolested by other races, and I await the Lizard King's command dispatching many of their forces to my command, that we may go establish supremacy in the Valley of Storms. Once she witnesses my conquests, Julia will have no choice but to accept me into her good graces.
